Simple habits like waking up early, limiting distractions (for example social media), and allocating specific time blocks for study or practice turn intentions into results. Consistency is more powerful than occasional effort; steady daily work compounds into skill, knowledge, and opportunities over months and years.\n\nWasting time leads to missed chances, stress, and regret. When we delay important tasks, problems pile up and quality suffers. In contrast, valuing time brings discipline, reduces anxiety, and builds confidence because tasks are completed and goals are met. Time also teaches respect for others—being punctual shows consideration and strengthens trust.\n\nUltimately, treating time as valuable helps us live a purposeful life. It encourages us to invest in things that matter—education, health, relationships, and honest work—so that when we look back, we see a life shaped by thoughtful choices rather than by avoidable losses.",

        "question": "Write a composition on [math]\\textbf{Floods in Bangladesh}[/math] in 250 words.",
        "solution": "[math]\\textbf{Floods in Bangladesh}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E [math]\\textbf{Introduction:}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E Bangladesh is one of the most flood-prone countries in the world. Its geographical position, numerous rivers, and monsoon climate make it vulnerable to frequent floods. Although floods are natural, their impact on people and the economy can be devastating.[math]\\textbf{Causes of Flood:}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E Heavy rainfall during the monsoon is the main cause of floods. Overflowing of rivers like Padma, Jamuna, and Brahmaputra submerges vast areas. Melting of Himalayan glaciers increases river water levels. Poor drainage in urban areas and deforestation make floods worse.[math]\\textbf{Effects of Floods:}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E Floods damage crops, houses, roads, schools, and hospitals. Many people become homeless and have to take shelter in flood centers. Food and drinking water become scarce. Diseases like diarrhea, cholera, and skin infections spread easily. Educational activities are interrupted for weeks.[math]\\textbf{Impact on Economy and Society:}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E Farmers suffer the most because their crops are washed away. Transportation stops, and business activities decline. Relief work becomes expensive and often delays. It is a common problem in Bangladesh, especially during the summer. It creates serious problems in homes, schools, offices, and hospitals.[math]\\textbf{Causes:}[/math]\u003Cbr\u003E The main cause is the shortage of electricity production. Other causes include misuse of electricity, old equipment, and poor management.         "explanation": "Load shedding refers to the planned, temporary interruption of electrical power supply to certain areas to prevent a total collapse of the power grid when demand exceeds available generation. It is typically used as an emergency measure when generation capacity, fuel supply, transmission constraints, or maintenance shortfalls make it impossible to meet peak demand. The immediate effects are widespread: households lose lighting and refrigeration, businesses halt production, schools and hospitals face disruptions, and public safety can be compromised. Repeated outages erode productivity, increase costs for businesses (through lost work and damaged equipment), and reduce the quality of life for residents.\n\nRoot causes include inadequate generation capacity, aging infrastructure, fuel shortages, poor maintenance, financial problems in power utilities, and weak grid management. Short-term coping strategies include scheduled outage notices, rotating supply to distribute inconvenience, backup generators, and community cooling/storage centers. Long-term solutions focus on increasing and diversifying supply (building new plants, investing in renewables like solar and wind), improving grid infrastructure and maintenance, strengthening transmission lines, implementing demand-side management (energy efficiency, time-of-use tariffs, smart meters), and reforming utility finances and governance to ensure reliable fuel procurement and investment.\n\nEffective policies combine technical upgrades with realistic planning and public communication so outages are minimized and better managed. Encouraging rooftop solar, battery storage, and microgrids can reduce peak pressure on the central grid and provide resilience for critical services. Ultimately, ending chronic load shedding requires sustained investment, transparent management, and coordinated energy policy that balances supply expansion with smarter demand management.",

There were already quotas for other groups, which meant only 44% of jobs were left for general applicants. He should make the illiterate literate. He can make the farmers aware of the modern methods of cultivation. In population control, he can play an important role.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nA student must obey and honour his parents. When they are sick, helpless or old, he must serve them. He should also be obedient to his teachers and other superiors.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nA student must not waste his time and energy. So he must possess a sound health by taking regular physical exercise, taking part in games and sports.         "solution": "\u003Cdiv style=\"text-align:center\"\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EThe Birds of Bangladesh\u003C/strong\u003E\u003C/div\u003E\nBangladesh is endowed with many natural gifts. Its climate, soil, marshes, rivers, canals, bills, haors, green fields, forests all have made it a suitable and ideal home for various kinds of birds to live in. From dawn to dusk we see many kinds of birds here and there. Their difference in colour, size and nature fascinates us.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe cuckoo, the doel, the bau-katha-kao, the shama, the moyna, the koel are prominent singing birds of Bangladesh. The cuckoo is the most popular of all singing birds. It appears at the advent of the spring. The doel is our national bird.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nAnother familiar bird in our country is the crow. When it caws at dawn, we know that the night is over. It is very clever but its voice is harsh and it looks ugly. It steals foods. It is very unpopular. Very often sitting upon electric wires or trees it empties its bowel upon passer-by.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe dove, the pigeon, the heron, the partridge, the goose are some common birds of Bangladesh. Their meat is tasty and delicious. The sparrow is another common bird.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe parrot and the moyna are talking birds. They can imitate the voice of man. So some people keep them as pets.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe kite, the hawk and the vulture are the birds of prey. They prey upon chickens and ducklings. The crane and the kingfisher are found near watery places. They live on fish. The woodpecker is a pretty bird with a strong bill. These birtis have keen eyes and sharp nails.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe birds of our country are our valuable assets. In many respects they are helpful to us. Many of them help in spreading the seeds of trees in different places. Thus they help in afforestation. Some of them eat up rubbish and many harmful insects and worms. Others add to the beauty of Nature. So we should not kill birds.         "question": "Floods in Bangladesh",
        "solution": "\u003Cdiv style=\"text-align: center;\"\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EFloods in Bangladesh\u003C/strong\u003E\u003C/div\u003E\nFlood means overflow of water. Bangladesh, being a land of rivers, often falls victims to floods almost every year. When it takes place seriously, it weakens our hopes of prosperity. It is devastating and horrible at it causes a colossal loss to lives and properties. It is like a curse of nature on us.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nHeavy rainfall often causes flood. Blockage of water also causes flood. In our country, flood is caused mainly due to heavy rainfall, blockage of water and release of too much water from the Farakka Barrage. Flood may also be caused by cyclones, tidal bores or melting of ice of mountains.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nFloods cause great havocs and sufferings to millions of people. Houses and cattle are washed away. Crops are damaged and many lives and properties are lost. Streets and roads go under water. People cannot go from one place to another. It makes rich people poor and poor people distressed.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe after effect of flood is very dangerous. Diarrhoea and other water-borne diseases break out after a flood. There is a scarcity of food and pure drinking water all around. The areas affected by flood become muddy and unhealthy. The prices of all daily necessary goods go up.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe government tries to take proper steps for the sufferers. Some voluntary organisations and NGOs help the affected people. They provide relief goods, medicines etc to them.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nIt is not an easy task to check floods. Firstly, drainage system should be improved. Secondly, river beds should be dredged. Thirdly, a well planned irrigation system should be introduced. Fourthly, we should build our houses on high land.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nFlood has some good sides too. Silt scatters on lands and it makes the soil fertile. Sometimes various kinds of crops grow more on these fertile lands. Then we get bumper crops.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nFlood is usually a great curse to us. It destroys our hopes and aspirations. Long term measures should be taken to control floods.\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cstrong\u003EWord meaning:\u003C/strong\u003E&nbsp;occur - ঘটা; seriously - মারাত্মকভাবে; prosperity - উন্নতি; devastating - বিধ্বংসী; horrible - ভয়ানক; colossal - বিশাল; on us - আমাদের ওপর; almost every year - প্রায় প্রতিবছর; weaken - দুর্বল করা; curse - অভিশাপ; heavy rainfall - ভারি বৃষ্টিপাত; blockage - প্রতিবন্ধকতা; farakka barrage - ফারাকা বাঁধ; sufferings - দুর্ভোগ; cattle - গবাদি পশু; water-bome - পানিবাহী; scarcity of food - খাদ্যাভাব; drinking water - খাবার পানি; muddy - কর্দমাক্ত; voluntary - স্বেচ্ছাসেবী; relief goods - ত্রাণ; scatter - ছড়িয়ে পড়া; long-term - দীর্ঘ মেয়াদী; due to - কারণে; havoc - ধ্বংস; washed away - ভাসিয়ে নেওয়া; properties - সম্পত্তি; after effect of flood - বন্যা পরবর্তী প্রভাব; break out - প্রাদুর্ভাব হওয়া; pure - বিশুদ্ধ; affected by flood - বন্যাক্রান্ত; go up - বেড়ে যাওয়া; affected people - আক্রান্ত লোকজন; silt - পলিমাটি; fertile - উর্বর; aspiration - উচ্চাশা; measure - পদক্ষেপ।",

Spring is one of them. It is the best and the most charming of all the seasons. The Bangla months of Falgun and Chaitra make this season. I like this season most.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nAmong the seasons, the spring occupies a very high position. To me the winter is very cold, dull and lifeless. In summer, the scorching sun, hot days and nights make life miserable. The heavy rain and frequent floods in the&nbsp;rainy season bring great sufferings for us. The autumn and the late autumn have more or less the disadvantages of the rainy season and the winter respectively. But the spring has none of the inconveniences of these seasons. Coming after winter, it captivates the hearts of all.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nWith the arrival of the spring, nature puts on a lively look. Everything of nature looks fresh. The sky looks clear and blue, trees put forth new leaves, flowers of charming colour and scent bloom in trees. Bees and butterflies hum and fly from one flower to another. During this season, gentle breeze begins to blow. Sweet twitters of birds are heard. The melodious notes of the cuckoo please our ears.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nAll these charming and pleasing sights and sounds have a positive influence on our mind. Everywhere there is joy and mirth. People enjoy a better health. They are happier in this season. Besides, various kinds of vegetables and fruits are also available in this time.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe season lasts for a very short period. During this season, some people suffer from some diseases like diarrhoea, cholera, chicken-pox. Pox is a common disease in this season.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nIn spite of its few disadvantages, its advantages are more. Truly speaking, its actual stay in Bangladesh is not more than two or three weeks. Perhaps its short stay has made it dearer to us. For all these reasons, I like spring most.\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cstrong\u003EWord meaning:\u003C/strong\u003E&nbsp;spring - বসন্তকাল; dull and lifeless - বিষা এবং প্রাণহীন; scorching sun - প্রখর রোদ; miserable - দুর্বিসহ/দুঃসহনীয়; flood - বন্যা ; suffering - ভোগান্তি; disadvantage - অসুবিধা; inconvenience - অসুবিধা/বিড়ম্বনা/কষ্ট/পীড়া; captivate - বিমোহিত/বিমুগ্ধ/সম্মোহিত করা; nature looks fresh - প্রকৃতিকে সতেজ দেখায়; sky looks clear and blue - আকাশ পরিষ্কার এবং নীল দেখায়; trees put forth new leaves - গাছে গাছে নতুন পাতা গজায়; melodious - সুরেলা; cuckoo - কোকিল; joy and mirth - আনন্দ এবং আমোদ-আহ্লাদ; diseases - রোগজীবাণু/রোগ/অসুখ; in spite of - সত্ত্বেও।",

        "solution": "\u003Cdiv style=\"text-align:center\"\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EThe Rivers of Bangladesh\u003C/strong\u003E\u003C/div\u003E\nBangladesh is a land of rivers. They have a great influence on our national and economic life. We get good benefits from them.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nOur main rivers are the Padma, the Meghna, the Jamuna, and the Karnaphuli. The Karnaphuli issues from the Lusai Mountains, the other rivers issue from the&nbsp;Himalayas and they all flow into the Bay of Bengal. All these rivers have their branches and tributaries. They spread over the country as a network. Thus these rivers give a new identity to our country as riverine Bangladesh.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe rivers are very useful to our life. They are helpful to our agriculture. We use our river water to irrigate our land. We can store river water during the rainy season and use them in dry season. We can also use the current of these rivers for producing electricity. They are important for water-way communication. They are the sources of fish. Many people lead their lives by catching and selling fish got from rivers.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nThe people of Bangladesh are greatly influenced by the rivers. The art and culture of our people are also influenced by them. Many poets have written poems on the rivers. Many of our people earn their livelihood from rivers.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nHowever, our rivers are also responsible for floods that destroy our economy. Again, in winter season the rivers get dry. Thus, it causes a serious problem to our agriculture. Bangladesh has more than 230 rivers. They are the gifts of nature. We should take proper steps to get more benefits from them. We should dredge them timely and properly.\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cbr /\u003E\n\u003Cstrong\u003EWord meaning\u003C/strong\u003E:&nbsp;great influence - ব্যাপক প্রভাব; national and economic - জাতীয় এবং অর্থনৈতিক; good benefits - ভালো উপকার; lusai mountains - লুসাই পর্বত; the other rivers issue from the himalyas - অন্যান্য নদীর উৎস হচ্ছে হিমালয়; all flow into the Bay of Bengal - সবগুলোই বঙ্গোপসাগরে পতিত হয়; spread over the country - দেশে ছড়িয়ে ছিটিয়ে আছে; riverine Bangladesh - নদীমাতৃক বাংলাদেশ; helpful for our agriculture - আমাদের কৃষির জন্য উপকারী; dry season - শুষ্ক মৌসুম; producing electricity - বিদ্যুৎ উৎপাদনে; current of these rivers - নদীর স্রোত; communication - যোগাযোগ; sources of fish - মাছের উৎস; by catching and selling fish - মাছ ধরে এবং বিক্রি করে; many of our people - আমাদের অনেক লোক; earn their livelihood from rivers - নদী দ্বারা জীবিকা নির্বাহ করে; responsible for floods - বন্যার জন্য দায়ী; destroy our economy - আমাদের অর্থনীতি ধ্বংস করে; gifts of nature - প্রকৃতির উপহার; proper step - যথাযথ পদক্ষেপ; dredge - নদী বা সমুদ্রের তলদেশ থেকে কর্দমাদি তোলার যন্ত্র; timely and properly - যথাসময়ে এবং যথাযথভাবে।",

Nearby villagers go to a village fair to buy various things. It gives them much joy and merriment.\u003Cbr /\u003E\nA village fair sits to celebrate the occasions like the first day of Baishakh and Muharram, the first month of the Hijri year etc. It sits under a big tree or at a suitable place of some villages.
